Insert log table entries in l_promotion_budgets, l_ad_tie_ups, l_promotion_descriptions and l_promotion_cv_links for the id to delete.
Note: Delete will not do anything if there are no log table entries for the id to delete.
While in tinker do Delete DB query for m_promotion_budgets, m_ad_tie_ups, m_promotion_descriptions and m_promotion_cv_links
Sample Test Data and Results:
Tinker command:
DB::delete("DELETE FROM migrate_afb2webridge.m_promotion_budgets WHERE (id = '1');")
